The Three Root Causes Framework\n\nBachmeyer's foundational model identifies **three systemic biological failures** that drive ALL chronic disease and aging:\n\n### Failure 1: Systemic Inflammation (\"The Forest Fire\")\n\n- **NOT** localized inflammation (swollen ankle, carpal tunnel)\n- A silent, body-wide blaze — the immune system is \"confused and exhausted\"\n- Decades of junk food, stress, and toxins cause it to go \"completely rogue\"\n- Dumps inflammatory cytokines: **IL-6, TNF-alpha** onto tissues\n- Burns artery linings, torches brain cells, destroys the nervous system\n- Creates a \"playground for cancer\"\n- This is **inflammaging** — the hallmark of every major age-related disease\n\n### Failure 2: Insulin Resistance (\"The Locked Door\")\n\n- Cells have gone \"completely deaf\" to insulin\n- Insulin (the key to unlock cells for glucose entry) is knocking, but the lock is jammed with **intramuscular fat and inflammation**\n- Pancreas overproduces insulin in response\n- Sugar ravages the bloodstream, glycating proteins, shredding capillaries\n- Root of: Type 2 diabetes, Alzheimer's (\"Type 3 diabetes\"), PCOS, fatty liver, dementia, MS\n\n### Failure 3: ATP Shortage (\"The Power Outage\")\n\n- Adenosine triphosphate (ATP) = the currency for ALL life functions\n- Every heartbeat, thought, cellular repair, blink, breath requires ATP\n- Mitochondria (the \"nuclear reactors\") are battered, inefficient, leaking toxic reactive oxygen species (ROS)\n- Producing less energy = **energetically bankrupt**\n- \"You're not tired because you're old. You're tired because your cellular economy is in a depression.\"\n\n### The Managed Decline Critique\n\n- Each symptom gets a pill; each pill has side effects requiring another pill\n- \"Pharmaceutical merry-go-round\" — the only one profiting is pharma\n- A 2020 JAMA Internal Medicine study showed polypharmacy in elderly (>53) is a disaster\n- Statins cause muscle wasting and cognitive decline; Metformin causes B12 deficiency\n- \"A healthy person is a lost customer\"\n\n---\n\n## 3. Core Peptide Protocols\n\n### 3.1 BPC-157 — \"The Forever Peptide\"\n\n| Parameter | Protocol |\n|-----------|----------|\n| **Classification** | Systemic repair / anti-inflammatory / \"the firefighter\" |\n| **Source** | Derived from protective stomach protein (15 amino acids) |\n| **Standard Dose** | 500 mcg SubQ daily (from X/Twitter post) |\n| **Injury Protocol** | 1 mg at site of injury every day for 14 days (Wolverine Protocol) |\n| **Daily Forever Dose** | 1 mg every day for life (Podcast Ep. 285) |\n| **Total Required (standard)** | 5 mg minimum |\n| **Administration** | SubQ injection ONLY — site-specific for injuries, belly fat for systemic |\n| **Cycling** | NO cycling — \"forever peptide,\" \"you don't cycle health\" |\n| **Needle** | 29-gauge insulin needle |\n| **Oral** | Absolutely NOT — destroyed by proteolytic enzymes and liver metabolism |\n\n**Mechanism of Action:**\n- Master regulator of the VEGF system — orchestrates precise angiogenesis\n- Promotes eNOS (endothelial nitric oxide synthase) → improved blood flow\n- Suppresses iNOS (inducible nitric oxide synthase) → reduces inflammatory damage\n- Promotes angiogenesis via HIF-1 alpha and VEGF axis\n- TGF-beta 1 agonist → collagen production\n- Increases nitric oxide → vasodilation\n- Crosses blood-brain barrier; upregulates growth hormone receptor\n- Modulates inflammation: reduces TNF-alpha, IL-6; promotes IL-10\n- Repairs intestinal tight junctions (leaky gut)\n- NF-kappa B pathway suppression\n\n**Clinical Applications:**\n- Tendon, ligament, bone, nerve repair\n- Cardiovascular healing (reduces infarct size, fibrosis)\n- Hepatic protection against toxins\n- Neurological recovery (nerve regeneration, spinal cord injury, TBI)\n- Lung fibrosis reversal\n- Gut lining repair\n- Blood-brain barrier protection\n\n### 3.2 MOTS-c — \"The Mitochondrial Commander\"\n\n| Parameter | Protocol |\n|-----------|----------|\n| **Classification** | Metabolic/mitochondrial optimization, insulin sensitizer |\n| **Source** | Encoded in mitochondrial DNA |\n| **Dose** | 5-10 mg SubQ, 2-3 times per week |\n| **Timing** | Fasted, before training (ideally first thing in morning) |\n| **Cycle** | 12 weeks on, 4 weeks off |\n| **Can run forever** | Yes — mentioned as safe for long-term use |\n| **Administration** | SubQ injection |\n\n**Mechanism of Action:**\n- Activates AMPK pathway (\"the cell's CFO\") in muscle tissue\n- Restores insulin sensitivity — makes cells \"beg for glucose\"\n- Optimizes folate cycle and purine biosynthesis\n- Builds the machinery inside mitochondria (\"the factory that builds the factory\")\n- Forces fatty acid oxidation — \"incinerating fat for fuel\"\n- Mimics exercise at the cellular level\n- Enhances cellular stress resilience\n\n**Critical Warning:**\n- Can cause **paradoxical fatigue** if mitochondria are already inflamed\n- Overstimulation of AMPK → oxidative burst → ATP depletion\n- Requires **mitochondrial preparedness** before use\n\n### 3.3 Epitalon — \"The Genetic Mechanic\"\n\n| Parameter | Protocol |\n|-----------|----------|\n| **Classification** | Anti-aging Stacking Protocols\n\n### 4.1 The \"Top 4 Forever\" Stack (Foundation)\n\nThe four peptides Bachmeyer would take if he could only choose four for the rest of his life:\n\n| # | Peptide | Role | Targets |\n|---|---------|------|---------|\n| 1 | MOTS-c | Metabolic command | Failure 2 (insulin resistance) + Failure 3 (ATP) |\n| 2 | Epitalon | Genetic renewal | Failure 1 (inflammation) + Failure 3 (ATP) |\n| 3 | BPC-157 | Systemic repair / firefighter | Failure 1 (inflammation) + all systems |\n| 4 | Thymosin Alpha-1 | Immune intelligence | Failure 1 (inflammation) |\n\n### 4.2 The \"Trilogy for Life\" / \"Biggest Bang for Your Buck\"\n\nThe three most cost-effective compounds:\n\n| # | Compound | Role |\n|---|----------|------|\n| 1 | BPC-157 | Healing — \"reinforced chassis\" |\n| 2 | MOTS-c | Performance — \"nitrous boost\" |\n| 3 | Methylene Blue | Cognition — \"turbo engine\" |\n\nSynergy: BPC-157 uses the ATP surplus from Methylene Blue to repair micro-damage. MOTS-c channels energy to burn fat and boost performance. Creates a \"closed-loop system of energy, metabolism, and resilience.\"\n\n### 4.3 The Wolverine Protocol (Injury Healing)\n\nFor acute/chronic injuries — three compounds:\n\n| # | Peptide | Role | Dose | Duration |\n|---|---------|------|------|----------|\n| 1 | BPC-157 | Signal caller — \"fix this NOW\" | 1 mg/day at injury site | 14 days minimum |\n| 2 | TB-500 | Foreman — regeneration | 5 mg every 5 days, belly fat | 4-6 weeks |\n| 3 | GHK-Cu | Finisher — quality control | 300 mcg/day, belly fat | 4-6 weeks |\n\n**Key rules:**\n- BPC-157 goes at the injury SITE, not the belly\n- TB-500 and GHK-Cu are systemic — inject into belly fat\n- Can mix TB-500 and GHK-Cu in same syringe (but different daily schedules)\n- Do NOT stop when pain stops — complete 4-6 weeks\n- Combine with smart rehab/movement — \"this is an amplifier, not invincibility juice\"\n\n### 4.4 The Mega Regeneration Stack\n\nFor full-system rejuvenation:\n\nBPC-157 + TB-500 + KPV + GHK-Cu + Tesamorelin/Ipamorelin\n\n\"Creates a synergistic full-system youth-restoring regeneration event from the cellular level up.\"\n\n### 4.5 Top 5 Peptides (Podcast Ep. 239)\n\n| # Cycling Guidelines\n\n| Peptide | Cycling Protocol |\n|---------|-----------------|\n| BPC-157 | No cycling needed — \"forever peptide\" (daily use for life) |\n| MOTS-c | 12 weeks on, 4 weeks off (or run forever at lower frequency) |\n| Epitalon | 20 days on, then 3-6 months off (2-3x per year) |\n| KPV | 4-6 weeks on, 2-4 weeks off (prevents receptor downregulation) |\n| TB-500 | 4 weeks loading → maintenance indefinitely |\n| GHK-Cu | 8-12 weeks on, then pulse |\n| RAD-140 | 8-12 weeks on, 2-4 weeks off |\n| Cardarine | 8-12 weeks on, 2-4 weeks off |\n| 5-Amino-1MQ | Can run long-term/forever |\n| Thymosin Alpha-1 | Daily (protocol duration unspecified — implied long-term) |\n\n**On the \"5 days on, 2 days off\" question:** Bachmeyer has a dedicated Rumble video addressing this — the answer depends on the specific peptide and its receptor dynamics.\n\n**General principle:** \"You don't cycle health. Administration & Injection Technique\n\n### Route Hierarchy\n\n| Route | Bachmeyer's Stance |\n|-------|-------------------|\n| SubQ injection | **PRIMARY and preferred** for all peptides |\n| Site-specific SubQ | Required for BPC-157 when treating injuries |\n| IM injection | Not emphasized — SubQ is sufficient |\n| Oral | \"Will NEVER work\" for peptides (see Section 8) |\n| Nasal | Acceptable for some compounds (e.g., Semax) |\n| Topical | Acceptable for KPV, GHK-Cu for skin conditions |\n| IV/drip | Criticizes NAD+ drips as wasteful — oral NMN + 5-Amino-1MQ better |\n\n### Injection Specifics\n\n- **Needle:** 29-gauge insulin needle (available on Amazon)\n- **Site-specific (BPC-157):** Inject SubQ within a few inches of injury site\n  - Elbow injury → inject near elbow (avoid ulnar nerve)\n  - Knee injury → inject near knee\n  - Knuckle, ankle, ear — wherever the injury is\n- **Systemic (TB-500, GHK-Cu, Thymosin Alpha-1, MOTS-c):** \"Grab a pinch of belly fat, fire it in\"\n- **Speed:** Inject slowly — never rush\n- **Rotation:** Rotate injection sites to prevent irritation\n\n### DMSO\n\n- Bachmeyer discusses DMSO as \"a potent, versatile, and underappreciated compound\"\n- \"Alleviates pain, reduces inflammation, and enhances drug delivery\"\n- Has a dedicated podcast episode (Ep. 241)\n- SLU-PP-332 available with or without DMSO on Elite Biogenix\n\n---\n\n## 7. Reconstitution & Storage\n\n### Reconstitution\n\n1. Use **1 mL of bacteriostatic water** per vial\n2. Do NOT use tap water or toilet water (his words)\n3. If no other choice, boil water for **20 minutes** (microwave does NOT count)\n4. Drop water into vial **gently** — aim for the side of the vial\n5. Do NOT shake — **swirl gently between your hands** (\"treat it like a newborn\")\n6. Peptides are \"fragments\" — they are fragile\n\n### Storage\n\n- **After reconstitution:** Refrigerate immediately\n- **Never freeze** reconstituted peptides\n- **Shelf life after reconstitution:** Up to 30 days refrigerated (with bacteriostatic water)\n- **Pre-reconstitution (lyophilized):** Can store frozen or refrigerated long-term\n\n---\n\n## 8. Oral vs Injectable — His Definitive Stance\n\n**Bachmeyer is unequivocal: oral peptides DO NOT WORK.**\n\nKey quotes and arguments:\n- \"Oral Peptides Will Never Work\" (dedicated podcast episodes: #168, #258, #307)\n- \"BUNK\" — oral peptides are worthless\n- BPC-157 is \"made in the stomach\" but cannot be taken orally\n- Proteolytic enzymes, stomach acid, and hepatic (liver) metabolism destroy peptides before absorption\n- \"Show me your blood work\" — his challenge to anyone claiming oral peptides work\n- \"If you challenge it, show me the blood work. I'll stop there till I see your blood work match somebody that takes it SubQ.\"\n- Nasal sprays and other delivery methods also fail for most peptides\n- The only exceptions: some compounds are designed for oral use (RAD-140, 5-Amino-1MQ, NMN, Cardarine, Methylene Blue, Semax nasal)\n\n---\n\n## 9. Cancer & Contraindications Stance\n\n### BPC-157 and Cancer\n\nBachmeyer is emphatic that BPC-157 **does NOT cause cancer:**\n\n- \"No study ever has linked BPC-157 to cancer. None. Not even correlated.\"\n- BPC-157's angiogenic effects are \"reparative and controlled\" — distinct from \"chaotic angiogenesis of tumors which is like spaghetti\"\n- \"It promotes orderly, controlled healing guided by the body's natural regulatory systems\"\n- Inhibits cancer cell growth and migration; promotes apoptosis\n\n### MOTS-c and Epitalon\n\n- \"By optimizing metabolism and reducing genomic instability, they create a hostile environment for cancer\"\n- Cancer \"thrives on glycolytic chaos\" — these peptides eliminate that chaos\n\n### Thymosin Alpha-1\n\n- \"Clinically used to help cancer patients fight their disease by boosting immune competence\"\n- \"Suggesting Thymosin Alpha-1 can do anything remotely close to causing cancer is medically illiterate\"\n- FDA-approved as adjunctive therapy for melanoma and Hepatitis B\n\n### General Stance\n\n- \"These compounds build a biology that is inherently resistant to cancer\"\n- The stack makes the body \"inhospitable to pathology\"\n- Fear-mongering about cancer \"is based on ignorance\"\n\n### Contraindications Mentioned\n\n- MOTS-c can cause **paradoxical fatigue** if mitochondria are already inflamed (need mitochondrial preparedness)\n- Retatrutide: GI slowdown, dehydration, electrolyte crashes, temporary insulin resistance spikes\n- PT-141: Nausea and flushing (\"you look like a tomato\") if dose is too high\n- Methylene Blue: Must be cycled to avoid toxicity; hormetic (low dose good, high dose harmful)\n- No dependency, drop-off, failure, or addiction with peptides: \"It doesn't work like that\"\n\n---\n\n## 12.
